<h2 id="purpose-and-scope" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Purpose and Scope<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h2>
<p>L2T (Language 2 Translate) is a command-line translation system that 
leverages the NLLB-200 (No Language Left Behind) neural machine 
translation model to provide translation capabilities across 200+ 
languages. This document provides a high-level overview of the system's 
architecture, components, and functionality. For installation 
instructions, see <a href="https://deepwiki.com/OlivierLAVAUD/L2T/2-installation-and-setup" class="text-neutral-300 hover:text-neutral-200 hover:underline">Installation and Setup</a>; for usage instructions, see <a href="https://deepwiki.com/OlivierLAVAUD/L2T/3-command-line-interface" class="text-neutral-300 hover:text-neutral-200 hover:underline">Command-Line Interface</a>.</p>
<h2 id="system-overview" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">System Overview<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h2>
<p>L2T is structured as a modular command-line application that allows 
users to translate text directly or from files, with support for both 
text files and PDFs. The system handles language detection, translation,
 and output generation through a pipeline of specialized components.</p>

<h2 id="core-components" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Core Components<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h2>
<h3 id="translation-cli" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Translation CLI<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>The <code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">TranslationCLI</code>
 class serves as the central orchestrator for the translation process. 
It processes command-line arguments, validates inputs, manages the 
translation workflow, and handles output generation.</p>
<h3 id="translation-engine" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Translation Engine<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>The <code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">NLLBTranslator</code>
 class implements the core translation functionality using the NLLB-200 
model. It provides methods for translating text, checking language 
support, and retrieving available languages.</p>
<h3 id="file-handlers" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">File Handlers<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>The <code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">FileHandler</code>
 class manages reading from and writing to different file formats, 
including text files and PDFs. It abstracts away the complexity of 
dealing with different file types.</p>
<h3 id="utilities" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Utilities<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<ul>
<li><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">TextProcessor</code>: Handles text manipulation tasks such as chunking text into manageable segments for translation</li>
<li><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">ProgressHandler</code>: Manages progress visualization during translation</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="logger" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Logger<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>Provides logging capabilities throughout the system for tracking operations and troubleshooting.</p>

<h2 id="command-line-interface" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Command-Line Interface<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h2>
<p>L2T provides a rich command-line interface with various options for controlling the translation process:</p>

<p>The CLI supports the following operations:</p>
<ul>
<li>Translating text strings directly</li>
<li>Translating text files</li>
<li>Translating PDF documents</li>
<li>Specifying source and target languages</li>
<li>Controlling output destination</li>
<li>Setting performance parameters (chunk size, batch size)</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="dependencies" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Dependencies<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>L2T relies on several key technologies:</p>
<ul>
<li>PyTorch: For neural network operations</li>
<li>Transformers library: To load and run the NLLB-200 model</li>
<li>PyPDF2: For PDF file processing</li>
<li>Accelerate: For optimized model inference</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="language-support" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Language Support<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h3>
<p>The system supports over 200 languages through the NLLB-200 model, using language codes in the format <code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">xxx_Latn</code> (e.g., <code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">eng_Latn</code> for English, <code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">fra_Latn</code> for French).</p>
<h2 id="file-structure" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">File Structure<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h2>
<p>The codebase follows a clean, modular organization:</p>





































<table><thead><tr><th>File</th><th>Purpose</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/main.py</code></td><td>Entry point for the application</td></tr><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/cli.py</code></td><td>Command-line interface implementation</td></tr><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/translator.py</code></td><td>Translation engine using NLLB-200</td></tr><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/file_handlers.py</code></td><td>File reading and writing operations</td></tr><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/utils.py</code></td><td>Text processing and progress visualization</td></tr><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/logger.py</code></td><td>Logging configuration</td></tr><tr><td><code class="rounded-sm bg-[#e5e5e5] px-[0.25rem] py-[0.20rem] text-xs font-normal leading-[15px] before:hidden after:hidden dark:bg-[#484848]/30">app/__init__.py</code></td><td>Package initialization</td></tr></tbody></table>

<h2 id="example-usage" class="group flex items-center" data-header="true">Example Usage<button class="relative ml-2 cursor-pointer text-gray-400 opacity-0 transition-opacity hover:text-blue-400 focus:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Copy link to header"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="h-4 w-4"><path d="M117.18,188.74a12,12,0,0,1,0,17l-5.12,5.12A58.26,58.26,0,0,1,70.6,228h0A58.62,58.62,0,0,1,29.14,127.92L63.89,93.17a58.64,58.64,0,0,1,98.56,28.11,12,12,0,1,1-23.37,5.44,34.65,34.65,0,0,0-58.22-16.58L46.11,144.89A34.62,34.62,0,0,0,70.57,204h0a34.41,34.41,0,0,0,24.49-10.14l5.11-5.12A12,12,0,0,1,117.18,188.74ZM226.83,45.17a58.65,58.65,0,0,0-82.93,0l-5.11,5.11a12,12,0,0,0,17,17l5.12-5.12a34.63,34.63,0,1,1,49,49L175.1,145.86A34.39,34.39,0,0,1,150.61,156h0a34.63,34.63,0,0,1-33.69-26.72,12,12,0,0,0-23.38,5.44A58.64,58.64,0,0,0,150.56,180h.05a58.28,58.28,0,0,0,41.47-17.17l34.75-34.75a58.62,58.62,0,0,0,0-82.91Z"></path></svg></button></h2>
<p>The system can be used in various ways, as demonstrated by the following examples:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Translate a text string to French:</p>
<pre class="px-2 py-1.5 has-[code]:rounded-md has-[code]:!bg-[#e5e5e5] has-[div]:bg-transparent has-[div]:!p-0 has-[code]:text-stone-900 dark:has-[code]:!bg-[#242424] has-[code]:dark:text-white [&amp;_code]:block [&amp;_code]:border-none [&amp;_code]:bg-transparent [&amp;_code]:p-0"><pre style="display: block; overflow-x: auto; padding: 6px 8px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: transparent; margin: 0px; width: 100%;"><code style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12px;"><span>uv </span><span style="color: rgb(0, 134, 179);">run</span><span> -m app.main </span><span style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">"Text to translate"</span><span> -l fra_Latn</span></code></pre></pre>
</li>
<li>
<p>Translate a text string from French to English:</p>
<pre class="px-2 py-1.5 has-[code]:rounded-md has-[code]:!bg-[#e5e5e5] has-[div]:bg-transparent has-[div]:!p-0 has-[code]:text-stone-900 dark:has-[code]:!bg-[#242424] has-[code]:dark:text-white [&amp;_code]:block [&amp;_code]:border-none [&amp;_code]:bg-transparent [&amp;_code]:p-0"><pre style="display: block; overflow-x: auto; padding: 6px 8px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: transparent; margin: 0px; width: 100%;"><code style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12px;"><span>uv </span><span style="color: rgb(0, 134, 179);">run</span><span> -m app.main </span><span style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">"Texte à traduire"</span><span> -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn</span></code></pre></pre>
</li>
<li>
<p>Translate a file and save the output:</p>
<pre class="px-2 py-1.5 has-[code]:rounded-md has-[code]:!bg-[#e5e5e5] has-[div]:bg-transparent has-[div]:!p-0 has-[code]:text-stone-900 dark:has-[code]:!bg-[#242424] has-[code]:dark:text-white [&amp;_code]:block [&amp;_code]:border-none [&amp;_code]:bg-transparent [&amp;_code]:p-0"><pre style="display: block; overflow-x: auto; padding: 6px 8px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: transparent; margin: 0px; width: 100%;"><code style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12px;"><span>uv </span><span style="color: rgb(0, 134, 179);">run</span><span> -m app.main my_file_to_translate.txt -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn -o my_translated_file.txt</span></code></pre></pre>
</li>
<li>
<p>Translate a PDF document:</p>
<pre class="px-2 py-1.5 has-[code]:rounded-md has-[code]:!bg-[#e5e5e5] has-[div]:bg-transparent has-[div]:!p-0 has-[code]:text-stone-900 dark:has-[code]:!bg-[#242424] has-[code]:dark:text-white [&amp;_code]:block [&amp;_code]:border-none [&amp;_code]:bg-transparent [&amp;_code]:p-0"><pre style="display: block; overflow-x: auto; padding: 6px 8px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); background: transparent; margin: 0px; width: 100%;"><code style="white-space: pre; font-size: 12px;"><span>uv run -m app.main docs/</span><span class="hljs-module-access hljs-module hljs-identifier">Le_Petit_Prince_ASE</span><span class="hljs-module-access hljs-module">.</span><span>pdf -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn</span></code></pre></pre>
</li>
</ol>
<p>Sources: <a href="https://github.com/OlivierLAVAUD/L2T/blob/0e4ae90a/README.md#L15-L37" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="mb-1 mr-1 inline-flex items-stretch font-mono text-xs !no-underline transition-opacity hover:opacity-75"><span class="flex items-center break-all rounded-l px-2 py-1.5 bg-[#e5e5e5] text-[#333333] dark:bg-[#252525] dark:text-[#e4e4e4]"><svg class="mr-1.5 Overview\n\n\u003cdetails\u003e\n\u003csummary\u003eRelevant source files\u003c/summary\u003e\n\nThe following files were used as context for generating this wiki page:\n\n- [README.md](README.md)\n- [app/README.md](app/README.md)\n- [app/__init__.py](app/__init__.py)\n\n\u003c/details\u003e\n\n\n\n## Purpose and Scope\n\nL2T (Language 2 Translate) is a command-line translation system that leverages the NLLB-200 (No Language Left Behind) neural machine translation model to provide translation capabilities across 200+ languages. This document provides a high-level overview of the system's architecture, components, and functionality. For installation instructions, see [Installation and Setup](#2); for usage instructions, see [Command-Line Interface](#3).\n\n## System Overview\n\nL2T is structured as a modular command-line application that allows users to translate text directly or from files, with support for both text files and PDFs. The system handles language detection, translation, and output generation through a pipeline of specialized components.\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n    User[\"User\"] --\u003e CLI[\"TranslationCLI\"]\n    CLI --\u003e Translator[\"NLLBTranslator\"]\n    CLI --\u003e FileHandlers[\"FileHandler\"]\n    CLI --\u003e TextProcessor[\"TextProcessor\"]\n    CLI --\u003e ProgressHandler[\"ProgressHandler\"]\n    \n    FileHandlers --\u003e PDF[\"PDF Processing\"]\n    FileHandlers --\u003e TXT[\"Text File Processing\"]\n    \n    Translator --\u003e NLLB[\"NLLB-200 Model\"]\n    \n    Main[\"main.py\"] --\u003e CLI\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py](), [app/translator.py](), [app/file_handlers.py](), [app/utils.py](), [app/logger.py](), [app/main.py]()\n\n## Core Components\n\n### Translation CLI\n\nThe `TranslationCLI` class serves as the central orchestrator for the translation process. It processes command-line arguments, validates inputs, manages the translation workflow, and handles output generation.\n\n### Translation Engine\n\nThe `NLLBTranslator` class implements the core translation functionality using the NLLB-200 model. It provides methods for translating text, checking language support, and retrieving available languages.\n\n### File Handlers\n\nThe `FileHandler` class manages reading from and writing to different file formats, including text files and PDFs. It abstracts away the complexity of dealing with different file types.\n\n### Utilities\n\n- `TextProcessor`: Handles text manipulation tasks such as chunking text into manageable segments for translation\n- `ProgressHandler`: Manages progress visualization during translation\n\n### Logger\n\nProvides logging capabilities throughout the system for tracking operations and troubleshooting.\n\nSources: [app/__init__.py:1-4](), [README.md:3-13]()\n\n## Translation Workflow\n\nThe following diagram illustrates the step-by-step process of translation in L2T:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"User Input\"] --\u003e B{\"Input Type?\"}\n    B --\u003e|\"Text String\"| C[\"Process Text Input\"]\n    B --\u003e|\"File Path\"| D[\"Determine File Type\"]\n    \n    D --\u003e|\"Text File\"| E[\"Read Text File\"]\n    D --\u003e|\"PDF File\"| F[\"Extract Text from PDF\"]\n    \n    E --\u003e G[\"Process Content\"]\n    F --\u003e G\n    C --\u003e G\n    \n    G --\u003e H{\"Source Language\\nSpecified?\"}\n    H --\u003e|\"Yes\"| I[\"Use Specified Source\"]\n    H --\u003e|\"No\"| J[\"Auto-detect Source Language\"]\n    \n    I --\u003e K[\"Translate to Target Language\"]\n    J --\u003e K\n    \n    K --\u003e L{\"Output Type?\"}\n    L --\u003e|\"Console\"| M[\"Print to Console\"]\n    L --\u003e|\"File with Path\"| N[\"Write to Specified File\"]\n    L --\u003e|\"Auto-generated\"| O[\"Create .T2L.txt File\"]\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py](), [app/translator.py](), [app/file_handlers.py](), [app/utils.py]()\n\n## Command-Line Interface\n\nL2T provides a rich command-line interface with various options for controlling the translation process:\n\n```mermaid\nclassDiagram\n    class TranslationCLI {\n        +run()\n        -_parse_arguments()\n        -_validate_arguments()\n        -_display_supported_languages()\n        -_load_content()\n        -_translate_content()\n        -_translate_in_chunks()\n        -_handle_output()\n        -_generate_output_path()\n    }\n```\n\nThe CLI supports the following operations:\n- Translating text strings directly\n- Translating text files\n- Translating PDF documents\n- Specifying source and target languages\n- Controlling output destination\n- Setting performance parameters (chunk size, batch size)\n\nSources: [README.md:15-37](), [app/README.md:15-52]()\n\n## Technical Specifications\n\n### System Components Relationship\n\nThe following diagram illustrates the relationships between the main classes in the L2T system:\n\n```mermaid\nclassDiagram\n    class TranslationCLI {\n        +run()\n        -_parse_arguments()\n        -_validate_arguments()\n        -_display_supported_languages()\n        -_load_content()\n        -_translate_content()\n    }\n    \n    class NLLBTranslator {\n        +translate()\n        +translate_batch()\n        +is_language_supported()\n        +get_supported_languages()\n        +load_model()\n    }\n    \n    class FileHandler {\n        +read_file()\n        +write_output()\n        -_read_pdf()\n        -_read_text_file()\n    }\n    \n    class TextProcessor {\n        +chunk_text()\n        +split_paragraphs()\n    }\n    \n    class ProgressHandler {\n        +display_progress()\n    }\n    \n    TranslationCLI --\u003e NLLBTranslator: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e FileHandler: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e TextProcessor: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e ProgressHandler: uses\n```\n\n### Dependencies\n\nL2T relies on several key technologies:\n- PyTorch: For neural network operations\n- Transformers library: To load and run the NLLB-200 model\n- PyPDF2: For PDF file processing\n- Accelerate: For optimized model inference\n\n### Language Support\n\nThe system supports over 200 languages through the NLLB-200 model, using language codes in the format `xxx_Latn` (e.g., `eng_Latn` for English, `fra_Latn` for French).\n\n## File Structure\n\nThe codebase follows a clean, modular organization:\n\n| File | Purpose |\n|------|---------|\n| `app/main.py` | Entry point for the application |\n| `app/cli.py` | Command-line interface implementation |\n| `app/translator.py` | Translation engine using NLLB-200 |\n| `app/file_handlers.py` | File reading and writing operations |\n| `app/utils.py` | Text processing and progress visualization |\n| `app/logger.py` | Logging configuration |\n| `app/__init__.py` | Package initialization |\n\nSources: [README.md:3-13](), [app/README.md:3-13]()\n\n## Example Usage\n\nThe system can be used in various ways, as demonstrated by the following examples:\n\n1. Translate a text string to French:\n   ```bash\n   uv run -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l fra_Latn\n   ```\n\n2. Translate a text string from French to English:\n   ```bash\n   uv run -m app.main \"Texte à traduire\" -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n   ```\n\n3. Translate a file and save the output:\n   ```bash\n   uv run -m app.main my_file_to_translate.txt -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn -o my_translated_file.txt\n   ```\n\n4. Translate a PDF document:\n   ```bash\n   uv run -m app.main docs/Le_Petit_Prince_ASE.pdf -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n   ```\n\nSources: [README.md:15-37](), [app/README.md:15-52]()"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"19:T1ab3,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# Installation and Setup\n\n\u003cdetails\u003e\n\u003csummary\u003eRelevant source files\u003c/summary\u003e\n\nThe following files were used as context for generating this wiki page:\n\n- [.python-version](.python-version)\n- [app/pyproject.toml](app/pyproject.toml)\n- [pyproject.toml](pyproject.toml)\n- [requirements.txt](requirements.txt)\n\n\u003c/details\u003e\n\n\n\nThis document outlines the steps required to install and configure the L2T (Language 2 Translate) system on your local machine. L2T is a command-line translation tool that leverages the NLLB-200 model to provide translation capabilities for over 200 languages.\n\nFor information about using the system after installation, see [Command-Line Interface](#3).\n\n## System Requirements\n\n### Hardware Requirements\n\n| Component | Minimum | Recommended |\n|-----------|---------|-------------|\n| CPU | Multi-core processor | Modern multi-core processor |\n| RAM | 8 GB | 16+ GB |\n| Storage | 5 GB free space | 10+ GB free space |\n| GPU | Not required | NVIDIA GPU with CUDA support |\n\n### Software Requirements\n\n* Python 3.13 or newer\n* pip (Python package installer)\n* Git (optional, for cloning the repository)\n\nSources: [.python-version:1-1](), [pyproject.toml:6-6]()\n\n## Installation Workflow\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Install Python 3.13+\"] --\u003e B[\"Clone/Download L2T\"]\n    B --\u003e C[\"Install Dependencies\"]\n    C --\u003e D[\"Verify Installation\"]\n    D --\u003e E[\"Configure GPU Acceleration (Optional)\"]\n    \n    subgraph \"Setup Environment\"\n        A\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"Get Codebase\"\n        B\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"Install Requirements\"\n        C\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"Test Installation\"\n        D\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"Performance Setup\"\n        E\n    end\n```\n\nSources: [pyproject.toml:1-12](), [requirements.txt:1-4]()\n\n## Step 1: Install Python\n\nL2T requires Python 3.13 or newer. During installation, ensure you check \"Add Python to PATH\"\n3. Verify installation by running in your terminal:\n   ```bash\n   python --version\n   ```\n\n## Step 2: Obtain the L2T Code\n\n### Option A: Clone the Repository (Recommended)\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/OlivierLAVAUD/L2T.git\ncd L2T\n```\n\n### Option B: Download ZIP\n\n1. Download the repository as a ZIP file from GitHub\n2. Extract the contents\n3. Navigate to the extracted directory in your terminal\n\n## Step 3: Install Dependencies\n\nInstall all required packages using pip:\n\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\nThis will install the following packages:\n- accelerate (≥1.6.0)\n- pypdf2 (≥3.0.1)\n- torch (≥2.7.0)\n- transformers (≥4.51.3)\n\nSources: [requirements.txt:1-4](), [pyproject.toml:7-12]()\n\n## Step 4: Verify Installation\n\nRun a simple command to verify that L2T is functioning correctly:\n\n```bash\npython -m app.main --list-languages\n```\n\nThis command should display a list of supported languages, indicating that the system is properly installed and the NLLB-200 model is accessible.\n\n## Dependency Integration Map\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n    subgraph \"External Dependencies\"\n        A[\"torch\u003e=2.7.0\\nNeural network library\"] \n        B[\"transformers\u003e=4.51.3\\nHuggingFace models\"]\n        C[\"pypdf2\u003e=3.0.1\\nPDF processing\"]\n        D[\"accelerate\u003e=1.6.0\\nOptimize execution\"]\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"L2T Core Components\"\n        E[\"NLLBTranslator\\napp/translator.py\"]\n        F[\"FileHandler\\napp/file_handlers.py\"]\n        G[\"TranslationCLI\\napp/cli.py\"]\n        H[\"main.py\\nProgram entry point\"]\n    end\n    \n    A --\u003e E\n    B --\u003e E\n    D --\u003e E\n    C --\u003e F\n    \n    E --\u003e G\n    F --\u003e G\n    G --\u003e H\n```\n\nSources: [requirements.txt:1-4](), [pyproject.toml:7-12]()\n\n## GPU Configuration (Optional)\n\nFor improved translation performance, especially with large texts, you can configure L2T to use GPU acceleration.\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n1. NVIDIA GPU with CUDA support\n2. Appropriate NVIDIA drivers installed\n3. Compatible CUDA toolkit installed\n\n### GPU Setup Process\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Install NVIDIA Drivers\"] --\u003e B[\"Install CUDA Toolkit\"]\n    B --\u003e C[\"Install PyTorch with CUDA Support\"]\n    C --\u003e D[\"Verify GPU Detection\"]\n    D --\u003e E[\"Configure Batch Size for Optimal Performance\"]\n    \n    subgraph \"Driver Setup\"\n        A\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"CUDA Environment\"\n        B\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"PyTorch Configuration\"\n        C\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"Verification\"\n        D\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"L2T Optimization\"\n        E\n    end\n```\n\n### Verify GPU Support\n\nRun the following Python command to check if PyTorch can detect your GPU:\n\n```python\nimport torch\nprint(\"CUDA available:\", torch.cuda.is_available())\nprint(\"CUDA device name:\", torch.cuda.get_device_name(0) if torch.cuda.is_available() else \"N/A\")\n```\n\nIf your GPU is properly configured, you should see `CUDA available: True` and your GPU's name.\n\n### Optimizing GPU Usage\n\nWhen using L2T, you can specify the GPU batch size to optimize performance:\n\n```bash\npython -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l \"fra_Latn\" --batch-size 8\n```\n\nFor more details on performance optimization, see [Performance Optimization](#5).\n\n## Troubleshooting Common Installation Issues\n\n### Python Version Error\n\n**Problem**: Error indicating Python version is too old.\n\n**Solution**: Install Python 3.13 or newer and ensure it's in your PATH.\n\n### PyTorch GPU Detection Failure\n\n**Problem**: PyTorch doesn't detect your GPU.\n\n**Solution**:\n1. Verify NVIDIA drivers are correctly installed\n2. Ensure CUDA toolkit is compatible with your PyTorch version\n3. Reinstall PyTorch with the correct CUDA version:\n   ```bash\n   pip uninstall torch\n   pip install torch --extra-index-url https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cu118\n   ```\n\n### Model Download Issues\n\n**Problem**: Errors when downloading the NLLB-200 model.\n\n**Solution**:\n1. Check your internet connection\n2. Ensure you have sufficient disk space\n3. Run with debug flag for detailed error information:\n   ```bash\n   python -m app.main --list-languages --debug\n   ```\n\n## Environment Configuration Table\n\n| Configuration | Default Value | How to Modify | Notes |\n|---------------|--------------|---------------|-------|\n| CUDA Device | Auto-detected | `CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES` env var | Set to specific GPU index |\n| Model Cache | ~/.cache/huggingface | `TRANSFORMERS_CACHE` env var | Change model storage location |\n| Batch Size | 4 | `--batch-size` argument | Increase for faster GPU processing |\n| Chunk Size | 500 | `-c/--chunk-size` argument | Adjust based on available memory |\n\n## Next Steps\n\nNow that you have successfully installed L2T, refer to [Command-Line Interface](#3) for information on how to use the system for translation tasks and [Basic Usage Examples](#3.1) for common translation scenarios.\n\nSources: [pyproject.toml:1-12](), [requirements.txt:1-4]()"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"1a:T22bb,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# Command-Line Interface\n\n\u003cdetails\u003e\n\u003csummary\u003eRelevant source files\u003c/summary\u003e\n\nThe following files were used as context for generating this wiki page:\n\n- [README.md](README.md)\n- [app/cli.py](app/cli.py)\n- [app/main.py](app/main.py)\n\n\u003c/details\u003e\n\n\n\nThe L2T Command-Line Interface (CLI) provides a robust and flexible way to access the translation capabilities of the system. This document details how to use the CLI, covering all available options and arguments. For basic usage examples, see [Basic Usage Examples](#3.1). For detailed information about advanced configuration options, see [Advanced CLI Options](#3.2).\n\n## Overview\n\nThe L2T CLI allows users to translate text directly from the command line. It supports translating:\n- Text strings provided directly in the command\n- Text files (.txt)\n- PDF documents (.pdf)\n\nThe interface is designed to be intuitive while providing advanced options for fine-tuning the translation process.\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    A[\"User Input\"] --\u003e B[\"TranslationCLI\"]\n    B --\u003e C[\"Parse Arguments\"]\n    C --\u003e D{\"Input Type?\"}\n    D --\u003e|\"Text String\"| E[\"Direct Translation\"]\n    D --\u003e|\"File Path\"| F[\"Load File Content\"]\n    F --\u003e G[\"Extract Text\"]\n    E --\u003e H[\"Translate\"]\n    G --\u003e H\n    H --\u003e I{\"Output Type?\"}\n    I --\u003e|\"Console\"| J[\"Display Result\"]\n    I --\u003e|\"File\"| K[\"Write to File\"]\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:14-177](), [app/main.py:5-16]()\n\n## Basic Command Structure\n\nThe L2T system is invoked through the `app.main` module with the following general syntax:\n\n```\nuv run -m app.main [input] [options]\n```\n\nWhere:\n- `[input]` is either text to translate or a path to a file\n- `[options]` are various configuration parameters\n\n### Required Arguments\n\n| Argument | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `input` | Text string to translate or path to a file (.txt/.pdf) |\n| `-l, --lang` | Target language code (e.g., `eng_Latn` for English, `fra_Latn` for French) |\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:23-45]()\n\n## Command-Line Options\n\n### Core Options\n\n| Option | Description | Default |\n|--------|-------------|---------|\n| `-l, --lang` | Target language code (required) | None |\n| `-s, --source-lang` | Source language code (optional - auto-detected if not specified) | Auto-detect |\n| `-o, --output` | Output file path | Console output |\n| `--list-languages` | Display all supported languages | False |\n\n### Advanced Options\n\n| Option | Description | Default |\n|--------|-------------|---------|\n| `-e, --encoding` | File encoding for input/output | utf-8 |\n| `-c, --chunk-size` | Text segment size for chunked translation | 500 |\n| `--batch-size` | GPU batch size for translation | 8 |\n| `--debug` | Enable debug mode for detailed logging | False |\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:23-45]()\n\n## Command Flow\n\nThe following diagram illustrates how the L2T CLI processes a translation request:\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant User\n    participant TranslationCLI\n    participant NLLBTranslator\n    participant FileHandler\n    participant TextProcessor\n\n    User-\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: Execute command\n    TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: Parse arguments\n    TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: Validate arguments\n    \n    alt List languages\n        TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eNLLBTranslator: get_supported_languages()\n        NLLBTranslator--\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: language list\n        TranslationCLI--\u003e\u003eUser: Display languages\n    else Translate content\n        alt File input\n            TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eFileHandler: read_file()\n            FileHandler--\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: file content\n        else Text input\n            TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: Use input directly\n        end\n        \n        alt Small text\n            TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eNLLBTranslator: translate()\n            NLLBTranslator--\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: translated text\n        else Large text\n            TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eTextProcessor: split_paragraphs()\n            TextProcessor--\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: paragraph list\n            loop For each paragraph\n                TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eNLLBTranslator: translate()\n                NLLBTranslator--\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: translated paragraph\n                TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eTranslationCLI: Update progress\n            end\n        end\n        \n        alt Output to file\n            TranslationCLI-\u003e\u003eFileHandler: write_output()\n            FileHandler--\u003e\u003eUser: Created output file\n        else Console output\n            TranslationCLI--\u003e\u003eUser: Display translation\n        end\n    end\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:47-67](), [app/cli.py:98-171]()\n\n## Translation Process\n\nWhen translating text, the CLI implements different strategies based on the content size:\n\n1. **Small text fragments** (≤ chunk size): Direct translation in one operation\n2. **Large documents**: Split into paragraphs and translate each paragraph separately with progress display\n\nFor large documents, the CLI displays a progress bar to show translation status and estimated completion time.\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Input Content\"] --\u003e B{\"Size \u003e Chunk Size?\"}\n    B --\u003e|\"No\"| C[\"Direct Translation\"]\n    B --\u003e|\"Yes\"| D[\"Split into Paragraphs\"]\n    D --\u003e E[\"Initialize Progress Bar\"]\n    E --\u003e F[\"Process Paragraphs\"]\n    F --\u003e G[\"Update Progress\"]\n    G --\u003e H{\"More Paragraphs?\"}\n    H --\u003e|\"Yes\"| F\n    H --\u003e|\"No\"| I[\"Join Results\"]\n    C --\u003e J[\"Final Translation\"]\n    I --\u003e J\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:98-151]()\n\n## Output Handling\n\nThe CLI offers three ways to handle the translation output:\n\n1. **Console output**: When translating a text string without specifying an output file\n2. **User-specified file**: Using the `-o/--output` option to define the target file\n3. **Auto-generated file**: When translating a file without specifying an output, creates a file with `.T2L.txt` suffix\n\nFor auto-generated output files, the following naming convention is used:\n`{original_filename}.{target_language_code}.T2L.txt`\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:154-177]()\n\n## CLI Implementation Architecture\n\nThe CLI is implemented through several classes working together:\n\n```mermaid\nclassDiagram\n    class Main {\n        +main()\n    }\n    \n    class TranslationCLI {\n        +__init__()\n        +run()\n        -_parse_arguments()\n        -_validate_arguments()\n        -_display_supported_languages()\n        -_load_content()\n        -_translate_content()\n        -_translate_in_chunks()\n        -_handle_output()\n        -_generate_output_path()\n    }\n    \n    class NLLBTranslator {\n        +translate()\n        +translate_batch()\n        +is_language_supported()\n        +get_supported_languages()\n    }\n    \n    class FileHandler {\n        +read_file()\n        +write_output()\n    }\n    \n    class TextProcessor {\n        +split_paragraphs()\n        +chunk_text()\n    }\n    \n    class ProgressHandler {\n        +display_progress()\n    }\n    \n    Main --\u003e TranslationCLI: instantiates\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e NLLBTranslator: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e FileHandler: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e TextProcessor: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e ProgressHandler: uses\n```\n\nSources: [app/main.py:5-16](), [app/cli.py:14-21]()\n\n## Example Commands\n\nHere are some example commands to get started with the L2T CLI:\n\n### Basic Translation\n\nTranslate a text string from auto-detected language to French:\n```\nuv run -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l fra_Latn\n```\n\nTranslate a text string from English to French:\n```\nuv run -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l fra_Latn -s eng_Latn\n```\n\n### File Translation\n\nTranslate a text file from French to English:\n```\nuv run -m app.main path/to/file.txt -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n```\n\nTranslate a PDF file from French to English:\n```\nuv run -m app.main path/to/document.pdf -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n```\n\n### Output Options\n\nSave translation to a specific file:\n```\nuv run -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l eng_Latn -o output.txt\n```\n\nAuto-generate output file for a text file:\n```\nuv run -m app.main path/to/file.txt -l eng_Latn\n```\nThis will create `path/to/file.eng-Latn.T2L.txt`\n\n### Utility Commands\n\nList all supported languages:\n```\nuv run -m app.main --list-languages\n```\n\nGet help:\n```\nuv run -m app.main --help\n```\n\nSources: [README.md:15-37]()\n\n## Error Handling\n\nThe CLI implements robust error handling for various scenarios:\n\n- Invalid language codes\n- Missing input\n- File not found\n- Empty content\n- Translation errors\n- Keyboard interruption\n\nWhen errors occur, the CLI provides informative error messages. In debug mode, it also shows detailed stacktraces.\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:59-66](), [app/main.py:11-16]()\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\nThe CLI includes several optimizations for performance:\n\n1. **Chunked translation**: Large texts are split into paragraphs for more efficient processing\n2. **Progress tracking**: Real-time progress display with time estimation\n3. **Batch processing**: Configurable batch size for GPU optimization\n\nFor more information about performance optimization, see [Performance Optimization](#5).\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:98-151]()"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"1b:T17bb,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# Basic Usage Examples\n\n\u003cdetails\u003e\n\u003csummary\u003eRelevant source files\u003c/summary\u003e\n\nThe following files were used as context for generating this wiki page:\n\n- [README.md](README.md)\n- [app/cli.py](app/cli.py)\n- [app/minimal/README.md](app/minimal/README.md)\n\n\u003c/details\u003e\n\n\n\nThis page provides practical examples of how to use the L2T (Language 2 Translate) command-line translation tool. It covers common use cases including translating text strings, text files, and PDF documents. For advanced command-line options, see [Advanced CLI Options](#3.2).\n\n## Command Structure\n\nThe basic syntax for using L2T follows this pattern:\n\n```\nuv run -m app.main [input] -l [target_language] [options]\n```\n\nWhere:\n- `[input]` is either a text string or file path\n- `[target_language]` is the language code to translate into (required)\n- `[options]` are additional parameters\n\n### Getting Help and Listing Languages\n\nBefore translating, you may want to view available options or check supported languages:\n\n```bash\n# Display help information\nuv run -m app.main --help\n\n# List all supported languages\nuv run -m app.main --list-languages\n```\n\nSources: [README.md:17-21]()\n\n## Translating Text Strings\n\n### Basic Text Translation\n\nTo translate a text string to a specific language:\n\n```bash\nuv run -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l eng_Latn\n```\n\nThis will translate the provided text to English (Latin script) and display the result in the console.\n\n### Specifying Source Language\n\nFor more accurate translations, you can specify the source language:\n\n```bash\nuv run -m app.main \"Texte à traduire\" -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n```\n\nThis explicitly tells the system that the source text is in French, which may improve translation quality.\n\nSources: [README.md:26-27](), [app/cli.py:35]()\n\n## Translation Process Workflow\n\nThe following diagram illustrates the basic translation workflow:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    A[\"Input Text/File\"] --\u003e B[\"TranslationCLI._load_content()\"]\n    B --\u003e C{\"Is File?\"}\n    C --\u003e|\"Yes\"| D[\"FileHandler.read_file()\"]\n    C --\u003e|\"No\"| E[\"Use Input as Text\"]\n    D --\u003e F[\"Text Content\"]\n    E --\u003e F\n    F --\u003e G[\"TranslationCLI._translate_content()\"]\n    G --\u003e H{\"Content Length \u003c= chunk_size?\"}\n    H --\u003e|\"Yes\"| I[\"NLLBTranslator.translate()\"]\n    H --\u003e|\"No\"| J[\"TranslationCLI._translate_in_chunks()\"]\n    J --\u003e K[\"Process with Progress Bar\"]\n    I --\u003e L[\"Translated Text\"]\n    K --\u003e L\n    L --\u003e M[\"TranslationCLI._handle_output()\"]\n    M --\u003e N{\"Output File Specified?\"}\n    N --\u003e|\"Yes\"| O[\"FileHandler.write_output()\"]\n    N --\u003e|\"No\"| P[\"Print to Console\"]\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:47-171]()\n\n## Translating Files\n\n### Text File Translation\n\nTo translate a text file:\n\n```bash\nuv run -m app.main my_file_to_translate.txt -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n```\n\nThis will:\n1. Read the text file\n2. Translate from French to English\n3. Create an output file named `my_file_to_translate.T2L.txt`\n\n### PDF File Translation\n\nL2T can extract text from PDF files and translate it:\n\n```bash\nuv run -m app.main docs/Le_Petit_Prince_ASE.pdf -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n```\n\nThis translates the content of the PDF file from French to English and creates an output text file.\n\nSources: [README.md:30-36](), [app/cli.py:83-96]()\n\n## File Handling Implementation\n\n```mermaid\nclassDiagram\n    class \"TranslationCLI\" {\n        +_load_content() str\n        +_generate_output_path() Path\n    }\n    \n    class \"FileHandler\" {\n        +read_file(path, encoding) str\n        +write_output(text, path, encoding) void\n        -_read_pdf(path) str\n        -_read_text_file(path, encoding) str\n    }\n    \n    \"TranslationCLI\" --\u003e \"FileHandler\" : uses\n    \n    note for FileHandler \"Handles both text files and PDFs\"\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:83-96](), [app/cli.py:154-177]()\n\n## Output Options\n\nL2T provides three ways to handle the translation output:\n\n| Output Method | Command Example | Description |\n|---------------|----------------|-------------|\n| Console output | `uv run -m app.main \"Text to translate\" -l eng_Latn` | Displays translation in the terminal |\n| Specified file | `uv run -m app.main \"Text\" -l eng_Latn -o output.txt` | Saves to the specified file path |\n| Auto-generated file | `uv run -m app.main input.txt -l eng_Latn` | Creates `input.eng-Latn.T2L.txt` |\n\n### Output to Specified File\n\nYou can specify an output file with the `-o` or `--output` option:\n\n```bash\nuv run -m app.main \"Texte à traduire\" -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn -o my_translated_file.txt\n```\n\nThis will save the translation to the specified file rather than displaying it in the console.\n\n### Auto-Generated Output Files\n\nWhen translating a file without specifying an output, L2T automatically generates an output filename:\n\n```bash\nuv run -m app.main my_file_to_translate.txt -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn\n```\n\nThis creates a file named `my_file_to_translate.eng-Latn.T2L.txt` in the same directory as the input file.\n\nSources: [README.md:28-33](), [app/cli.py:154-177]()\n\n## Handling Large Files\n\nL2T processes large files by breaking them into chunks:\n\n1. The text is split into paragraphs\n2. Each paragraph is translated individually\n3. A progress bar displays translation progress\n4. Results are combined into a single output\n\nFor large files, you'll see a progress indicator that looks like this:\n```\nTranslation of 42 segments:\n[====================] 100% (42/42) - ETA: 0s - Elapsed: 15s\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:98-151]()\n\n## Common Use Case Patterns\n\n| Use Case | Example Command | Notes |\n|----------|----------------|-------|\n| Quick text translation | `uv run -m app.main \"Hello world\" -l fra_Latn` | Output to console |\n| Translating with known source | `uv run -m app.main \"Hello\" -l fra_Latn -s eng_Latn` | Better accuracy |\n| Translating a document | `uv run -m app.main document.txt -l eng_Latn` | Auto-generated output |\n| Custom output location | `uv run -m app.main input.txt -l deu_Latn -o output/result.txt` | Specific output path |\n| Translating a PDF | `uv run -m app.main document.pdf -l eng_Latn -s fra_Latn` | Extracts and translates text |\n\nSources: [README.md:24-37](), [app/minimal/README.md:6-14]()"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"1c:T1ff8,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# Advanced CLI Options\n\n\u003cdetails\u003e\n\u003csummary\u003eRelevant source files\u003c/summary\u003e\n\nThe following files were used as context for generating this wiki page:\n\n- [app/cli.py](app/cli.py)\n- [app/utils.py](app/utils.py)\n\n\u003c/details\u003e\n\n\n\nThis document provides detailed information about the advanced command-line options available in the L2T (Language 2 Translate) system. These options enable users to fine-tune the translation process, control output behavior, and optimize performance. For basic usage examples, refer to [Basic Usage Examples](#3.1).\n\n## Overview of Advanced Options\n\nL2T provides several advanced command-line options that allow users to customize various aspects of the translation process:\n\n| Option | Flag | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| Output file | `-o`, `--output` | Auto-generated | Specify output file path |\n| Encoding | `-e`, `--encoding` | utf-8 | Set file encoding |\n| Chunk size | `-c`, `--chunk-size` | 500 | Control text segment size for processing |\n| Batch size | `--batch-size` | 8 | Set GPU batch processing size |\n| Debug mode | `--debug` | Disabled | Enable verbose error reporting |\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:38-43]()\n\n## Text Processing Options\n\n### Chunk Size (`-c`, `--chunk-size`)\n\nThe chunk size option controls how the system divides longer texts into manageable segments for translation. This is crucial for:\n\n1. Efficient memory usage\n2. Progress tracking\n3. Preventing context loss in translation\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"large_document.txt\" -l fra_Latn -c 600\n```\n\nThis increases the default segment size from 500 to 600 characters. Optimal chunk sizes depend on your specific text and available memory:\n\n- **Smaller chunks** (200-400): Better for memory-constrained environments\n- **Larger chunks** (600-1000): May provide better context for translation but require more memory\n\nThe system automatically splits text by paragraphs and processes them as individual units.\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Input Text\"] --\u003e B[\"TextProcessor.split_paragraphs()\"]\n    B --\u003e C{\"Paragraph \u003e Chunk Size?\"}\n    C --\u003e|Yes| D[\"Further Chunking\"]\n    C --\u003e|No| E[\"Translate Paragraph\"]\n    D --\u003e E\n    E --\u003e F[\"Combine Results\"]\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:97-119](), [app/cli.py:123-151](), [app/utils.py:23-34]()\n\n## Performance Optimization\n\n### Batch Size (`--batch-size`)\n\nThe batch size parameter controls how many text chunks are processed simultaneously on the GPU. This directly impacts translation speed and memory usage.\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"large_document.pdf\" -l deu_Latn --batch-size 12\n```\n\nThis increases the batch size from the default 8 to 12 chunks, potentially improving throughput on systems with powerful GPUs.\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    A[\"Text Chunks\"] --\u003e B[\"Batch 1\\n(N chunks)\"]\n    A --\u003e C[\"Batch 2\\n(N chunks)\"]\n    A --\u003e D[\"...\"]\n    A --\u003e E[\"Batch M\\n(N chunks)\"]\n    \n    B --\u003e F[\"GPU Processing\"]\n    C --\u003e F\n    D --\u003e F\n    E --\u003e F\n    \n    F --\u003e G[\"Translated Text\"]\n```\n\nGuidelines for selecting batch size:\n- **Higher values**: Better GPU utilization, faster processing\n- **Lower values**: Lower memory usage, more suitable for systems with limited GPU memory\n- **When to adjust**: If you experience out-of-memory errors or want to maximize throughput\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:42]()\n\n## Output Configuration\n\n### Output File (`-o`, `--output`)\n\nBy default, L2T automatically generates output filenames with the pattern `{original_filename}.{language_code}.T2L.txt`. The `-o` option allows you to specify a custom output path:\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"input.txt\" -l spa_Latn -o \"spanish_translation.txt\"\n```\n\nIf the input is a string rather than a file and no output file is specified, the translation will be printed to the console.\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"translate command\"] --\u003e B{\"Output file\\nspecified?\"}\n    B --\u003e|Yes| C[\"Write to specified file path\"]\n    B --\u003e|No| D{\"Input is a file?\"}\n    D --\u003e|Yes| E[\"Generate auto-filename:\\n{input}.{lang}.T2L.txt\"]\n    D --\u003e|No| F[\"Display in console\"]\n    E --\u003e G[\"Write to file\"]\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:154-171](), [app/cli.py:172-177]()\n\n### File Encoding (`-e`, `--encoding`)\n\nThe encoding option allows you to specify the character encoding for both input and output files:\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"russian_text.txt\" -l eng_Latn -e \"windows-1251\"\n```\n\nThis is particularly useful when working with files in non-UTF-8 encodings, such as:\n- `windows-1252` for Western European languages\n- `windows-1251` for Cyrillic scripts\n- `ISO-8859-15` for European languages\n- `shift-jis` for Japanese\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:40]()\n\n## Debugging Options\n\n### Debug Mode (`--debug`)\n\nThe debug mode enables verbose error reporting, which is essential for diagnosing issues with translations:\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"problematic_file.txt\" -l ita_Latn --debug\n```\n\nWhen debug mode is enabled:\n1. Full exception traces are displayed in the console\n2. More detailed logging is provided\n3. Processing information becomes more verbose\n\nThis is particularly useful when:\n- A translation unexpectedly fails\n- You're experiencing issues with specific language pairs\n- You need to report a bug to the developers\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Error occurs\"] --\u003e B{\"Debug mode\\nenabled?\"}\n    B --\u003e|Yes| C[\"Log full exception\\ntrace and details\"]\n    B --\u003e|No| D[\"Log simplified error message\"]\n    C --\u003e E[\"Display to user\"]\n    D --\u003e E\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:43](), [app/cli.py:62-64]()\n\n## Advanced Usage Examples\n\n### Optimizing for Large Documents\n\nWhen translating large documents, you can combine chunk size and batch size adjustments for optimal performance:\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"large_book.pdf\" -l fra_Latn -c 800 --batch-size 16\n```\n\n### Working with Custom Encodings\n\nFor files with specific encoding requirements:\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"legacy_document.txt\" -l deu_Latn -e \"iso-8859-1\" -o \"output_utf8.txt\"\n```\n\nNote that the output will be in the specified encoding (in this case, iso-8859-1).\n\n### Debugging Translation Issues\n\nWhen experiencing problems with specific texts:\n\n```\npython -m app.main \"problematic_text.txt\" -l ara_Arab --debug\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:38-43]()\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\nThe choice of chunk size and batch size directly impacts system performance:\n\n| Parameter | Small Value | Large Value |\n|-----------|-------------|-------------|\n| Chunk Size | Lower memory usage\u003cbr\u003eMore translation requests\u003cbr\u003ePotentially reduced context | Better context preservation\u003cbr\u003eFewer translation requests\u003cbr\u003eHigher memory usage |\n| Batch Size | Lower GPU memory usage\u003cbr\u003ePotentially slower processing | Better GPU utilization\u003cbr\u003eFaster processing\u003cbr\u003eHigher GPU memory requirements |\n\nFor optimal performance:\n1. On systems with limited GPU memory, use smaller batch sizes\n2. For texts where context is important, use larger chunk sizes\n3. For large documents, ensure adequate disk space for output files\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TD\n    subgraph \"CLI Parameters\"\n        ChunkSize[\"chunk-size\\n-c option\"]\n        BatchSize[\"batch-size\\n--batch-size option\"]\n    end\n    \n    subgraph \"System Components\"\n        TextProcessor[\"TextProcessor.split_paragraphs()\"]\n        Translator[\"NLLBTranslator.translate()\"]\n        ProgressHandler[\"ProgressHandler.display_progress()\"]\n    end\n    \n    ChunkSize --\u003e TextProcessor\n    BatchSize --\u003e Translator\n    TextProcessor --\u003e Translator\n    Translator --\u003e ProgressHandler\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:97-119](), [app/cli.py:123-151](), [app/utils.py:5-22]()\n\n## Best Practices\n\n1. **Memory Management**: Start with default values and adjust if you encounter memory issues\n2. **File Encoding**: Always specify the correct encoding for input files to avoid character corruption\n3. **Batch Optimization**: On systems with powerful GPUs, increase batch size for better performance\n4. **Progress Monitoring**: For large documents, monitor the progress bar to estimate completion time\n5. **Error Handling**: Use debug mode when troubleshooting unexpected translation results\n\nBy leveraging these advanced options appropriately, you can optimize the L2T system for your specific translation needs and hardware capabilities.\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:38-43](), [app/utils.py:5-22]()"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"1d:T2610,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# diagram illustrates how the components interact during a typical translation operation:\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant User as \"User\"\n    participant CLI as \"TranslationCLI\"\n    participant FileHandler as \"FileHandler\"\n    participant NLLBTranslator as \"NLLBTranslator\"\n    participant TextProcessor as \"TextProcessor\"\n    participant ProgressHandler as is file\"\n        CLI-\u003e\u003eFileHandler: \"read_file()\"\n        FileHandler--\u003e\u003eCLI: \"content\"\n    else \"Input is text\"\n        Note over CLI: \"Use input text directly\"\n TranslationCLI\n\nThe `TranslationCLI` class acts as the central orchestrator of the translation process. It handles command-line arguments, coordinates between other components, and manages the overall translation workflow.\n\n#### Key Responsibilities:\n- Parsing and validating command-line arguments\n- Loading content from files or direct input\n- Managing the translation process\n- Handling output to console or files\n- Coordinating progress display for large texts\n\n#### Key Methods:\n\n| Method | Purpose |\n|--------|---------|\n| `run()` | Main entry point that orchestrates the full translation process |\n| `_parse_arguments()` | Configures and processes command-line arguments |\n| `_load_content()` | Loads text from input sources (files or direct input) |\n| `_translate_content()` | Manages the translation process with optimizations |\n| `_translate_in_chunks()` | Handles large text translation with progress display |\n| `_handle_output()` | Manages the output of translated content |\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:14-177]()\n\n### 2. NLLBTranslator\n\nThe `NLLBTranslator` class encapsulates the NLLB-200 neural machine translation model and provides methods for text translation.\n\n#### Key Responsibilities:\n- Loading and initializing the translation model\n- Performing text translation\n- Supporting batch translation for better performance\n- Maintaining a list of supported languages\n\n#### Key Methods:\n\n| Method | Purpose |\n|--------|---------|\n| `load_model()` | Initializes the NLLB-200 model with optimizations for GPU or CPU |\n| `translate()` | Translates a single text input to a target language |\n| `translate_batch()` | Translates multiple texts in batches for better performance |\n| `is_language_supported()` | Checks if a language is supported by the model |\n| `get_supported_languages()` | Returns the dictionary of supported language codes and names |\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:4-210]()\n\n### 3. FileHandler\n\nThe `FileHandler` class provides static methods for file operations, including reading from different file formats and writing translation results.\n\n#### Key Responsibilities:\n- Reading text content from files (plain text and PDF)\n- Writing translated content to output files\n- Handling file encoding\n\n#### Key Methods:\n\n| Method | Purpose |\n|--------|---------|\n| `read_file()` | Reads content from a file based on its format |\n| `_read_pdf()` | Extracts text from PDF files using PyPDF2 |\n| `_read_text_file()` | Reads text from plain text files with encoding support |\n| `write_output()` | Writes translated content to an output file |\n\nSources: [app/file_handlers.py:1-54]()\n\n### 4. Text Processing Utilities\n\n#### TextProcessor\n\nThe `TextProcessor` class provides utilities for processing text for translation.\n\n#### Key Methods:\n\n| Method | Purpose |\n|--------|---------|\n| `chunk_text()` | Breaks text into smaller chunks of a fixed size |\n| `split_paragraphs()` | Separates text into individual paragraphs |\n\n#### ProgressHandler\n\nThe `ProgressHandler` class provides utilities for displaying progress information during translation.\n\n#### Key Methods:\n\n| Method | Purpose |\n|--------|---------|\n| `display_progress()` | Shows a progress bar for translation operations |\n\nSources: [app/utils.py:1-34]()\n\n### 5. Logger\n\nThe logging module provides functions for consistent logging throughout the application.\n\n#### Key Functions:\n\n| Function | Purpose |\n|--------|---------|\n| `setup_logging()` | Configures the logging system with file and console outputs |\n| `log_execution_time()` | Records the execution time of operations |\n\nSources: [app/logger.py:1-29]()\n\n## Component Class Structure\n\nThe following class diagram illustrates the structure and relationships of the core components:\n\n```mermaid\nclassDiagram\n    class TranslationCLI {\n        +logger\n        +translator\n        +args\n        +start_time\n        +__init__()\n        +run()\n        -_parse_arguments()\n        -_validate_arguments()\n        -_display_supported_languages()\n        -_load_content()\n        -_translate_content()\n        -_translate_in_chunks()\n        -_handle_output()\n        -_generate_output_path()\n    }\n    \n    class NLLBTranslator {\n        +model\n        +tokenizer\n        +translator_pipe\n        +supported_languages\n        +_loaded\n        +load_model()\n        +translate()\n        +translate_batch()\n        +is_language_supported()\n TextProcessor {\n        +chunk_text()\n        +split_paragraphs()\n    }\n    \n    class ProgressHandler {\n        +display_progress()\n    }\n    \n    TranslationCLI --\u003e NLLBTranslator: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e FileHandler: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e TextProcessor: uses\n    TranslationCLI --\u003e ProgressHandler: uses\n```\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:14-177](), [app/translator.py:4-210](), [app/file_handlers.py:6-54](), [app/utils.py:5-34]()\n\n## Component Dependencies\n\n| Component | External Dependencies | Internal Dependencies |\n|-----------|----------------------|----------------------|\n| TranslationCLI | argparse, sys, time, datetime, pathlib | NLLBTranslator, FileHandler, TextProcessor, ProgressHandler, Logger |\n| NLLBTranslator | transformers, torch | None |\n| FileHandler | PyPDF2, pathlib | None |\n| TextProcessor | None | None |\n| ProgressHandler | sys, time | None |\n| Logger | logging, datetime | None design patterns:\n\n1. **Facade Pattern**: `TranslationCLI` acts as a facade, providing a simplified interface to the complex translation subsystem.\n\n2. **Static Utility Classes**: `FileHandler`, `TextProcessor`, and `ProgressHandler` are implemented as classes with static methods, functioning as utility libraries.\n\n3. **Lazy Loading**: The translation model is loaded only when needed, optimizing memory usage.\n\n4. **Command Pattern**: The CLI arguments effectively act as commands that control the behavior of the system.\n\n5. **Chain of Responsibility**: The translation process flows through a chain of methods, each handling a specific aspect of the process.\n\nSources: [app/cli.py:14-177](), [app/translator.py:113-146](), [app/file_handlers.py:6-54](), [app/utils.py:5-34]()"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"1e:T2268,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"# Translation Engine\n\n\u003cdetails\u003e\n\u003csummary\u003eRelevant source files\u003c/summary\u003e\n\nThe following files were used as context for generating this wiki page:\n\n- [app/minimal/cli-nllb.py](app/minimal/cli-nllb.py)\n- [app/minimal/test-nllb.py](app/minimal/test-nllb.py)\n- [app/translator.py](app/translator.py)\n\n\u003c/details\u003e\n\n\n\nThis document details the Translation Engine component of the L2T system, specifically covering the NLLB-200 (No Language Left Behind) model and its implementation within our translation architecture. For information about text processing before and after translation, see [Text Processing](#4.3). For information about file handling, see [File Handling](#4.2).\n\n## NLLB-200 Model Overview\n\nThe L2T system employs Meta AI's NLLB-200 model, a state-of-the-art neural machine translation system capable of translating between over 200 language pairs. The specific implementation uses the distilled 600M parameter version, which balances performance and resource requirements.\n\nKey features of the NLLB-200 model include:\n- Support for 200+ languages, many of which are low-resource languages\n- Transformer-based sequence-to-sequence architecture\n- Distilled model version for improved inference speed\n- Optimized for both CPU and GPU execution\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph \"Translation Engine Components\"\n        Model[\"NLLB-200 Model\"]\n        Tokenizer[\"NLLB Tokenizer\"]\n        Pipeline[\"Translation Pipeline\"]\n    end\n    \n    Text[\"Input Text\"] --\u003e Tokenizer\n    Tokenizer --\u003e Model\n    Model --\u003e Pipeline\n    Pipeline --\u003e Result[\"Translated Text\"]\n    \n    Language[\"Language Code (e.g., fra_Latn)\"] --\u003e Model\n```\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:122-131](). [app/minimal/test-nllb.py:4-5]()\n\n## NLLBTranslator Class Architecture\n\nThe translation engine is implemented through the `NLLBTranslator` class, which encapsulates all functionality related to the NLLB model.\n\n```mermaid\nclassDiagram\n    class NLLBTranslator {\n        -model: AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM\n        -tokenizer: AutoTokenizer\n        -translator_pipe: pipeline\n        -_loaded: bool\n        -supported_languages: dict\n        +load_model()\n        +translate(text, target_lang, source_lang)\n        +translate_batch(texts, target_lang, source_lang)\n        +get_supported_languages()\n        +is_language_supported(lang_code)\n    }\n```\n\nThe `NLLBTranslator` class manages:\n1. Model and tokenizer loading and configuration\n2. Single and batch translation operations\n3. Language support verification\n4. GPU/CPU execution optimization\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:4-179]()\n\n## Model Loading and Initialization\n\nThe model is loaded lazily when first needed through the `load_model()` method, which handles:\n\n1. Determining the appropriate device (GPU or CPU)\n2. Loading the model with optimized settings\n3. Configuring the tokenizer\n4. Setting up the translation pipeline\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    Start[\"Translation Request\"] --\u003e Loaded{\"Model Loaded?\"}\n    Loaded --\u003e|\"No\"| LoadModel[\"load_model()\"]\n    Loaded --\u003e|\"Yes\"| Translate[\"Perform Translation\"]\n    \n    LoadModel --\u003e CheckGPU{\"GPU Available?\"}\n    CheckGPU --\u003e|\"Yes\"| GPUSettings[\"Set float16 precision\"]\n    CheckGPU --\u003e|\"No\"| CPUSettings[\"Set float32 precision\"]\n    \n    GPUSettings --\u003e LoadComponents[\"Load Model \u0026 Tokenizer\"]\n    CPUSettings --\u003e LoadComponents\n    \n    LoadComponents --\u003e SetupPipeline[\"Configure Translation Pipeline\"]\n    SetupPipeline --\u003e Translate\n```\n\nThe initialization process automatically detects hardware capabilities and optimizes accordingly:\n\n| Hardware | Configuration | Benefits |\n|----------|--------------|----------|\n| GPU (CUDA) | float16 precision, device_map=\"auto\" | Faster processing, memory efficiency |\n| CPU only | float32 precision | Compatibility, stability |\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:113-145]()\n\n## Translation Operations\n\nThe system supports two primary translation methods:\n\n### 1. Single Text Translation\n\nThe `translate()` method handles individual text translation:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    Input[\"Input Text\"] --\u003e LoadCheck{\"Model Loaded?\"}\n    LoadCheck --\u003e|\"No\"| LoadModel[\"Load Model\"]\n    LoadCheck --\u003e|\"Yes\"| Device[\"Set Device (CPU/GPU)\"]\n    LoadModel --\u003e Device\n    \n    Device --\u003e Tokenize[\"Tokenize Text\"]\n    Tokenize --\u003e Generate[\"Generate Translation\"]\n    Generate --\u003e Decode[\"Decode Output Tokens\"]\n    Decode --\u003e Result[\"Translated Text\"]\n    \n    TargetLang[\"Target Language Code\"] --\u003e Generate\n    SourceLang[\"Optional Source Language\"] --\u003e Tokenize\n```\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:179-210]()\n\n### 2. Batch Translation\n\nThe `translate_batch()` method enables efficient batch processing:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    Inputs[\"List of Texts\"] --\u003e Pipe[\"Translation Pipeline\"]\n    SrcLang[\"Source Language Prefix\"] --\u003e Pipe\n    TgtLang[\"Target Language\"] --\u003e Pipe\n    BatchConfig[\"Batch Size \u0026 Beam Search\"] --\u003e Pipe\n    \n    Pipe --\u003e Results[\"List of Translated Texts\"]\n```\n\nPerformance parameters:\n- Batch size of 8 (configurable)\n- Beam search with 2 beams\n- Early stopping enabled\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:147-169]()\n\n## Language Handling\n\nThe translation engine supports over 100 languages through a defined mapping of language codes to readable names. Each language is identified by a code with the format `{language}_{script}`, such as:\n\n- `fra_Latn`: French (Latin script)\n- `zho_Hans`: Chinese (Simplified)\n- `ara_Arab`: Arabic (Arabic script)\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph \"Language Handling\"\n        Support[\"is_language_supported()\"]\n        GetLangs[\"get_supported_languages()\"]\n        LangDict[\"supported_languages dictionary\"]\n    end\n    \n    Input[\"Language Code (e.g., 'fra_Latn')\"] --\u003e Support\n    Support --\u003e|\"Check\"| LangDict\n    LangDict --\u003e|\"Return all\"| GetLangs\n    Support --\u003e|\"Yes/No\"| Result[\"Boolean Result\"]\n    GetLangs --\u003e FullList[\"Complete Language List\"]\n```\n\nSample of supported languages:\n\n| Language Code | Language Name |\n|---------------|---------------|\n| eng_Latn | English |\n| fra_Latn | French |\n| spa_Latn | Spanish |\n| deu_Latn | German |\n| zho_Hans | Chinese (Simplified) |\n| jpn_Jpan | Japanese |\n| ara_Arab | Arabic |\n| rus_Cyrl | Russian |\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:10-111](), [app/translator.py:171-177]()\n\n## Integration with L2T System\n\nThe Translation Engine interfaces with other components of the L2T system:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    CLI[\"TranslationCLI\"] --\u003e|\"Initializes\"| Translator[\"NLLBTranslator\"]\n    Translator --\u003e|\"Processes\"| TextProcessor[\"Text Processing\"]\n    TextProcessor --\u003e|\"Chunked Text\"| Translator\n    Translator --\u003e|\"Returns\"| OutputHandler[\"Output Handling\"]\n    \n    Translator --\u003e|\"load_model()\"| ModelInit[\"Model Initialization\"]\n    Translator --\u003e|\"translate() / translate_batch()\"| Translation[\"Translation Process\"]\n    \n    ModelInit --\u003e|\"Uses\"| HuggingFace[\"NLLB-200 Model\"]\n    Translation --\u003e|\"Uses\"| HuggingFace\n```\n\nKey integration points:\n1. The CLI component initializes the translator\n2. Text chunks from the text processing component are sent to the translator\n3. The translator returns translated content to the output handling system\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:4-210]()\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\nThe Translation Engine implements several optimizations:\n\n1. **GPU Acceleration**: Automatic detection and utilization of CUDA-enabled GPUs\n2. **Memory Efficiency**: Precision adjustment based on available hardware\n3. **Batch Processing**: Efficient handling of multiple texts in a single forward pass\n4. **Lazy Loading**: Model is only loaded when needed to conserve resources\n5. **Tokenizer Optimization**: Fast tokenizer implementation for improved processing speed\n\nFor more in-depth information about performance optimization, see [Performance Optimization](#5).\n\nSources: [app/translator.py:113-145](), [app/translator.py:147-169](), [app/translator.py:179-210]()\n\n## Basic Usage Example\n\nThe simplest implementation of the translation engine is demonstrated in the minimal test example:\n\n```python\nfrom transformers import AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM, AutoTokenizer\n\n# Load model and tokenizer\nmodel = AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained(\"facebook/nllb-200-distilled-600M\")\ntokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(\"facebook/nllb-200-distilled-600M\")\n\n# Text to translate\ntext = \"Hello world\"\n\n# Encode with target language code\ninputs = tokenizer(text, return_tensors=\"pt\")\n\n# Translate to French (fra_Latn)\ntranslated = model.generate(\n    **inputs,\n    forced_bos_token_id=tokenizer.convert_tokens_to_ids(\"fra_Latn\")\n)\n\n# Decode the result\nprint(tokenizer.decode(translated[0], skip_special_tokens=True))\n```\n\nSources: [app/minimal/test-nllb.py:1-20]()\n\nThe L2T system builds upon this core functionality with additional features like batch processing, language verification, device optimization, and integration with
